                  </form>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَسِيرُ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">سَيْرٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَسِيرٌ</foreign>, (S, M, A, Mgh, Msb, K,) which latter is extr., for by rule it should be of the measure <foreign lang="ar">مَفْعَلٌ</foreign>, with fet-h [to the <foreign lang="ar">ع</foreign>], (S,) and <foreign lang="ar">مَسِيرَةٌ</foreign> (M, K) and <foreign lang="ar">سَيْرُورَةٌ</foreign> (M, Mgh, K) like <foreign lang="ar">قَيْلُولَةٌ</foreign>, but [Mtr says] we have not heard it, (Mgh,) and <foreign lang="ar">تَسْيَارٌ</foreign>, (S, M, K,) which last denotes repetition or frequency of the action, (M,) <hi rend="ital">He,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, went</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in any manner,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">any pace</hi>]; <hi rend="ital">went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">passed, along; marched, journeyed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proceeded; went away, passed away,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">departed;</hi> (M, * K, * TA;) <hi rend="ital">by night</hi> and <hi rend="ital">by day.</hi> (Msb, TA.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">سَارَتِ الدَّابَّةُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The beast went, went along,</hi> &amp;c.]. (S.) [And <foreign lang="ar">سار سَيْرًا شَدِيدًا</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He</hi> (a camel or other beast, and a man,) <hi rend="ital">went a vehement pace,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">vehemently.</hi> And <foreign lang="ar">سار العَنَقَ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He</hi> (a camel, or a horse,) <hi rend="ital">went the pace,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">in the manner, termed</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">العَنَق</foreign>: and the like.] And <foreign lang="ar">سَارُوا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">مِنْ بَلَدٍ لِبَلَدٍ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">They went,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">journeyed, from town to town,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">from country to country</hi>]: (A:) or <foreign lang="ar">سار مِنْ بَلَدٍ إِلَى بَلَدٍ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">he went,</hi> &amp;c.]. (Mgh.) And <foreign lang="ar">بَارَكَ ٱللّٰهُ فِى مَسِيرِكَ</foreign> i. e. <foreign lang="ar">سَيْرِكَ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">May God bless thy journeying</hi>]. (S.) (Mgh.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">سار سِيرَةً حَسَنَةً</foreign> <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  [<hi rend="ital">He pursued a good way, course, mode,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">manner, of acting,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">conduct,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like</hi>], (S, A, Msb,) and <foreign lang="ar">سِيرَةً</foreign>

                  <foreign lang="ar">النَّاسِ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">It became current,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">commonly known, among the people;</hi> [as also

(M.)          <sense type="b" n="5">-b5-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">سارت سُنَّةٌ</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  [<hi rend="ital">A way, course, mode,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">manner, of acting,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">conduct,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like, obtained,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">was usual, among people</hi>].                   <foreign lang="ar">سَيَّرَ</foreign>. (S, M, Msb, K.) See the latter, in five places.          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">سار</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">سُنَّةً</foreign> <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">He made,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">caused, a way, course, mode,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">manner, of acting,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">conduct,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the like, to obtain,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became usual, among people.</hi> (S, M, * TA.)
